===========================
Question Name: Intro
===========================
Type: Text
---------------------------

[Pre-Skips]:
Pre-Skip: Skip from Intro to OverQuota ALWAYS SKIP

[Header 2]:
<p>Thank you for taking our survey on single-serve coffee machines.  We will be asking you a series of questions related to your preferences regarding coffee machines that use pods such as the Nespresso, Keurig, or Verismo.  The survey is for an academic research project and is not associated with any of the companies mentioned in the survey.  Your responses will assist us in investigating the ways in which a wide variety of products are marketed and sold and will be used to prepare a paper that will be submitted to a scientific journal.  
</p>
<p>The survey is completely confidential and we will not be collecting any personally identifying information. The entire survey should take no more than 15 minutes to complete.
</p>
<p>Please answer each question to the best of your ability.  There are no right or wrong answers; we are simply interested in your opinions and perceptions.  Use the right arrow button displayed on the bottom of the page to move to the next question.  This will ensure that your answers are properly recorded.  Do not use the “Back” or “Forward” buttons on your browser as this may disrupt the survey.  Your answers will be saved automatically when you click the right arrow button.  If you are interrupted while taking the survey you may come back and complete the survey by clicking on the original link you were sent.
</p>
<p>Please note that this survey has not been optimized for mobile devices.  While it may be possible to complete the survey on a smartphone or other small device, we recommend that you take the survey on a device with a larger screen.</p>

<p>Your participation in the survey is completely voluntary.  You may close your browser at any time and end the survey.
</p>
<p>If you have problems taking the survey please click the “Survey Support” link at the bottom of each page.  Alternatively you may contact John Howell of Penn State University at 814-867-4766 with any questions or concerns.  If you have questions regarding your rights as a research subject or concerns regarding your privacy, you may contact the Penn State Office for Research Protections at 814-865-1775.
</p>
<p>
By clicking the right arrow button you are consenting to participate in this research survey.  Please click the right arrow button to begin.
</p>

----------------------------------<PAGE BREAK>----------------------------------

===========================
Question Name: ConjointIntro
===========================
Type: Text
---------------------------

[Header 2]:
<p>On the following screens we will ask you about a hypothetical purchasing situation.  We are interested in understanding which machines and varieties of coffee you would consider purchasing. 
</p><p>
<b>On the following screens please assume that you are currently shopping for a single-serve coffee machine and that the presented options are the only products available to you.</b>
</p><p>
You will be asked to select between coffee machines and to provide an estimate for the number of cups of coffee that you would brew using that machine each week.  This exercise will be repeated a number of times.
</p><p>
While the screens may look similar, the product features and prices will change between each screen.  We need to ask you 12 questions in order to fully discover the nature of your preferences and understand your purchasing behavior as the products change.  Also note that some of the options shown may not currently be available in stores.  Please assume that they are and answer accordingly.
</p><p>
Please consider each question carefully so we can better understand what you would purchase.
</p>

----------------------------------<PAGE BREAK>----------------------------------

===========================
Question Name: Glossary
===========================
Type: Text
---------------------------

[Header 1]:
Glossary

[Header 2]:


<p>The pods are specific to each brand of machine.  For	example you will not be able to use Nespresso pods with a Keurig machine.</p>

<p>The machines are described based on the following features:
	<ul style="list-style-type: circle">
		<li><b>Brand</b> - This specifies who makes the machine as well as determining which type of pods can be used with the machine.</li>
		<li><b>Size of reservoir</b> - This determines how many cups of coffee you can make before having to refill the water in the machine. The size is expressed in both fluid ounces as well as the number of cups that can typically be made between refills.</li>
		<li><b>Cup Sizes</b> - Number of different sizes of cups that can be chosen - This describes how many different sizes of cups can be made. For example, the machine may be able to make a 10 oz. cup of coffee, a 20 oz. travel mug, and a carafe that can be used to serve guests. This would count as three different cup sizes. Different size cups may require a different number or size of pods. For purposes of this study please assume that a regular serving is 1 pod or 10 oz. of coffee and adjust your serving estimates accordingly.</li>
		<li><b>Brew Time</b> - Length of time required to brew a single 10 oz. cup</li>
		<li><b>Price</b> - The price of the machine</li>
	</ul>
</p>
<p>Because we are limited on space we are not able to perfectly describe each of the machines in detail.  Please assume that any features of the machine that are not explicitly mentioned are similar. For example, assume that all of the machines have touch controls, are equivalently easy to use, and all machines have the same 1 year warranty.
</p>
<p>In addition to the machines you will be asked to predict how many cups (or cup equivalents) of coffee you will make using your chosen machine.  The coffee pods are described based on the following features.
   <ul style="list-style-type: circle">
		<li><b>Brand</b> - This is the company that makes the coffee pods.  Each brand often makes multiple flavors or varieties of pods.  Please assume that all flavor varieties for that brand are available.</li>
		<li><b>Price per pod</b> - Prices range from $0.35 - $1.00 per pod. Please assume that the price per pod is the regular price and not a sale price.  The prices should remain stable over the life of the machine.</li>
   </ul>
</p>

===========================
Question Name: CBCRandom1
===========================
Type: Free Format
---------------------------

[Header 2]:
<p>Assuming that you were in the market to purchase a single-serve coffee machine and these were the only products available, which machine or machines would you purchase? (You may review the features of the machines by clicking [% PopUp("here", "Glossary.html", 600, 800) %].)</p>
<p>Please also indicate how many of each coffee pods or other cups of coffee you and members of your household would <span class="emphasis">consume</span> in a typical week. You can select a combination of pods, coffee shop purchases and home brew machines if that is what you would actually do. (Note that some of the coffee pods are only available for certain machines.) </p>
<p>Based on your answer to a previous question we estimate that you would have spent about <span style="text-decoration: underline">$[% FormatNumber(HeavyConsumption*0.65, ",", ".", 2)  %]</span> to purchase coffee using a pod based system on a week you drank more coffee than normal. </p>

[HTML <head> Tag]:
<script>	
function SSI_CustomGraphicalCheckbox(GraphicalCheckboxObj, InputObj, blnCheck) {
	var price = parseFloat($(InputObj).closest("div").find("h4").text().replace(/\$/g, ''))
	if(blnCheck) {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) + price;
	} else {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) - price;
	}
	$("#machineTotalPrice").text("$" + SSI_PriceFormat(newPrice, ",", ".").toString())

}

function updatePodPrices() {
	
	var spend = new Array();
	
	$.each($(":text"), function(index, value) {
		var quantity = parseFloat(($(value).val()));
		var price = parseFloat($(value).closest("li").find("input:hidden").val());
		spend[index] = quantity*price;
	});
	
	var totalSpend = 0;

	$.each(spend, function(index, value) {
		if(!isNaN(value)) {
			totalSpend += value;
		}
	});
	
	$("#podsTotalPrice").text("$" + totalSpend.formatMoney(",", ".", 2));
	
}

$(document).ready(function() {$(":text").change(updatePodPrices)})

$(function(){
 var keyStop = {
   8: ":not(input:text, textarea, input:file, input:password)", // stop backspace = back
   13: "input:text, input:password", // stop enter = submit 

   end: null
 };
 $(document).bind("keydown", function(event){
  var selector = keyStop[event.which];

  if(selector !== undefined && $(event.target).is(selector)) {
      event.preventDefault(); //stop event
  }
  return true;
 });
});


/**
 * Number.prototype.format(numDecimalDigits)
 * 
 * This breaks the nubmer down into parts. It strips out the
 * sign, the numbers before the first comma, the rest of the 
 * whole number portion, and the decimal part of the answer.
 */
Number.prototype.formatMoney = function(numDecimalDigits) {
	var number = this,
		numDecimalDigits = isNaN(numDecimalDigits) ? 2 : Math.abs(numDecimalDigits),
		thousandSeparator = ',',
		decimalSeparator = ".",
		sign = (number < 0) ? '-' : '',
		integerPart = parseInt(number = Math.abs(number).toFixed(numDecimalDigits)) + '',
		leadingDigits = (leadingDigits = integerPart.length) > 3 ? leadingDigits % 3 : 0;
   return sign + (leadingDigits ? integerPart.substr(0, leadingDigits) + thousandSeparator : "") + 
		integerPart.substr(leadingDigits).replace(/(\d{3})(?=\d)/g, "$1" + thousandSeparator) + 
		(numDecimalDigits ? decimalSeparator + Math.abs(number - integerPart).toFixed(numDecimalDigits).slice(2) : "");
};



</script>

[JavaScript Verification]:
Call Order: After other verification

for(i = 1; i <=3; i++) {
	var questionName = strQuestName + "_MachineChoice_" + i;
	
	var totalPods = 0;
	$("[id^=" + strQuestName + "_Concept" + i + "Pod]").each(function () { totalPods += parseFloat($(this).val()) || 0;})
	

	//If Machine is checked at least one pod must be purchased
	if(SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods <= 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase at least one pod to use the coffee machine you chose.";
	}

	//If a pods is purchased the machine must be checked
	if(!SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods > 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase the machine in order to use the pods you selected.";
	}
	
}

<p>Assuming that you were in the market to purchase a single-serve coffee machine and these were the only products available, which machine or machines would you purchase? (You may review the features of the machines by clicking [% PopUp("here", "Glossary.html", 600, 800) %].)</p>

[HTML <head> Tag]:
<script>	
function SSI_CustomGraphicalCheckbox(GraphicalCheckboxObj, InputObj, blnCheck) {
	var price = parseFloat($(InputObj).closest("div").find("h4").text().replace(/\$/g, ''))
	if(blnCheck) {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) + price;
	} else {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) - price;
	}
	$("#machineTotalPrice").text("$" + SSI_PriceFormat(newPrice, ",", ".").toString())

}

function updatePodPrices() {
	
	var spend = new Array();
	
	$.each($(":text"), function(index, value) {
		var quantity = parseFloat(($(value).val()));
		var price = parseFloat($(value).closest("li").find("input:hidden").val());
		spend[index] = quantity*price;
	});
	
	var totalSpend = 0;

	$.each(spend, function(index, value) {
		if(!isNaN(value)) {
			totalSpend += value;
		}
	});
	
	$("#podsTotalPrice").text("$" + totalSpend.formatMoney(",", ".", 2));
	
}

$(document).ready(function() {$(":text").change(updatePodPrices)})

$(function(){
 var keyStop = {
   8: ":not(input:text, textarea, input:file, input:password)", // stop backspace = back
   13: "input:text, input:password", // stop enter = submit 

   end: null
 };
 $(document).bind("keydown", function(event){
  var selector = keyStop[event.which];

  if(selector !== undefined && $(event.target).is(selector)) {
      event.preventDefault(); //stop event
  }
  return true;
 });
});


/**
 * Number.prototype.format(numDecimalDigits)
 * 
 * This breaks the nubmer down into parts. It strips out the
 * sign, the numbers before the first comma, the rest of the 
 * whole number portion, and the decimal part of the answer.
 */
Number.prototype.formatMoney = function(numDecimalDigits) {
	var number = this,
		numDecimalDigits = isNaN(numDecimalDigits) ? 2 : Math.abs(numDecimalDigits),
		thousandSeparator = ',',
		decimalSeparator = ".",
		sign = (number < 0) ? '-' : '',
		integerPart = parseInt(number = Math.abs(number).toFixed(numDecimalDigits)) + '',
		leadingDigits = (leadingDigits = integerPart.length) > 3 ? leadingDigits % 3 : 0;
   return sign + (leadingDigits ? integerPart.substr(0, leadingDigits) + thousandSeparator : "") + 
		integerPart.substr(leadingDigits).replace(/(\d{3})(?=\d)/g, "$1" + thousandSeparator) + 
		(numDecimalDigits ? decimalSeparator + Math.abs(number - integerPart).toFixed(numDecimalDigits).slice(2) : "");
};



</script>

[JavaScript Verification]:
Call Order: After other verification

for(i = 1; i <=3; i++) {
	var questionName = strQuestName + "_MachineChoice_" + i;
	
	var totalPods = 0;
	$("[id^=" + strQuestName + "_Concept" + i + "Pod]").each(function () { totalPods += parseFloat($(this).val()) || 0;})
	

	//If Machine is checked at least one pod must be purchased
	if(SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods <= 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase at least one pod to use the coffee machine you chose.";
	}

	//If a pods is purchased the machine must be checked
	if(!SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods > 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase the machine in order to use the pods you selected.";
	}
	
}

<p>Assuming that you were in the market to purchase a single-serve coffee machine and these were the only products available, which machine or machines would you purchase? (You may review the features of the machines by clicking [% PopUp("here", "Glossary.html", 600, 800) %].)</p>

You can select a combination of pods, coffee shop purchases and home brew machines if that is what you would actually do. (Note that some of the coffee pods are only available for certain machines.) </p>

[HTML <head> Tag]:
<script>	
function SSI_CustomGraphicalCheckbox(GraphicalCheckboxObj, InputObj, blnCheck) {
	var price = parseFloat($(InputObj).closest("div").find("h4").text().replace(/\$/g, ''))
	if(blnCheck) {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) + price;
	} else {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) - price;
	}
	$("#machineTotalPrice").text("$" + SSI_PriceFormat(newPrice, ",", ".").toString())

}

function updatePodPrices() {
	
	var spend = new Array();
	
	$.each($(":text"), function(index, value) {
		var quantity = parseFloat(($(value).val()));
		var price = parseFloat($(value).closest("li").find("input:hidden").val());
		spend[index] = quantity*price;
	});
	
	var totalSpend = 0;

	$.each(spend, function(index, value) {
		if(!isNaN(value)) {
			totalSpend += value;
		}
	});
	
	$("#podsTotalPrice").text("$" + totalSpend.formatMoney(",", ".", 2));
	
}

$(document).ready(function() {$(":text").change(updatePodPrices)})

$(function(){
 var keyStop = {
   8: ":not(input:text, textarea, input:file, input:password)", // stop backspace = back
   13: "input:text, input:password", // stop enter = submit 

   end: null
 };
 $(document).bind("keydown", function(event){
  var selector = keyStop[event.which];

  if(selector !== undefined && $(event.target).is(selector)) {
      event.preventDefault(); //stop event
  }
  return true;
 });
});


/**
 * Number.prototype.format(numDecimalDigits)
 * 
 * This breaks the nubmer down into parts. It strips out the
 * sign, the numbers before the first comma, the rest of the 
 * whole number portion, and the decimal part of the answer.
 */
Number.prototype.formatMoney = function(numDecimalDigits) {
	var number = this,
		numDecimalDigits = isNaN(numDecimalDigits) ? 2 : Math.abs(numDecimalDigits),
		thousandSeparator = ',',
		decimalSeparator = ".",
		sign = (number < 0) ? '-' : '',
		integerPart = parseInt(number = Math.abs(number).toFixed(numDecimalDigits)) + '',
		leadingDigits = (leadingDigits = integerPart.length) > 3 ? leadingDigits % 3 : 0;
   return sign + (leadingDigits ? integerPart.substr(0, leadingDigits) + thousandSeparator : "") + 
		integerPart.substr(leadingDigits).replace(/(\d{3})(?=\d)/g, "$1" + thousandSeparator) + 
		(numDecimalDigits ? decimalSeparator + Math.abs(number - integerPart).toFixed(numDecimalDigits).slice(2) : "");
};



</script>

[JavaScript Verification]:
Call Order: After other verification

for(i = 1; i <=3; i++) {
	var questionName = strQuestName + "_MachineChoice_" + i;
	
	var totalPods = 0;
	$("[id^=" + strQuestName + "_Concept" + i + "Pod]").each(function () { totalPods += parseFloat($(this).val()) || 0;})
	

	//If Machine is checked at least one pod must be purchased
	if(SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods <= 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase at least one pod to use the coffee machine you chose.";
	}

	//If a pods is purchased the machine must be checked
	if(!SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods > 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase the machine in order to use the pods you selected.";
	}
	
}

[Header 2]:
<p>Assuming that you were in the market to purchase a single-serve coffee machine and these were the only products available, which machine or machines would you purchase? (You may review the features of the machines by clicking [% PopUp("here", "Glossary.html", 600, 800) %].)</p>
<p>Please also indicate how many of each coffee pods or other cups of coffee you and members of your household would <span class="emphasis">consume</span> in a typical week. You can select a combination of pods, coffee shop purchases and home brew machines if that is what you would actually do. (Note that some of the coffee pods are only available for certain machines.) </p>
<p>Based on your answer to a previous question we estimate that you would have spent about <span style="text-decoration: underline">$[% FormatNumber(HeavyConsumption*0.65, ",", ".", 2)  %]</span> to purchase coffee using a pod based system on a week you drank more coffee than normal. </p>

[HTML <head> Tag]:
<script>	
function SSI_CustomGraphicalCheckbox(GraphicalCheckboxObj, InputObj, blnCheck) {
	var price = parseFloat($(InputObj).closest("div").find("h4").text().replace(/\$/g, ''))
	if(blnCheck) {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) + price;
	} else {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) - price;
	}
	$("#machineTotalPrice").text("$" + SSI_PriceFormat(newPrice, ",", ".").toString())

}

function updatePodPrices() {
	
	var spend = new Array();
	
	$.each($(":text"), function(index, value) {
		var quantity = parseFloat(($(value).val()));
		var price = parseFloat($(value).closest("li").find("input:hidden").val());
		spend[index] = quantity*price;
	});
	
	var totalSpend = 0;

	$.each(spend, function(index, value) {
		if(!isNaN(value)) {
			totalSpend += value;
		}
	});
	
	$("#podsTotalPrice").text("$" + totalSpend.formatMoney(",", ".", 2));
	
}

$(document).ready(function() {$(":text").change(updatePodPrices)})

$(function(){
 var keyStop = {
   8: ":not(input:text, textarea, input:file, input:password)", // stop backspace = back
   13: "input:text, input:password", // stop enter = submit 

   end: null
 };
 $(document).bind("keydown", function(event){
  var selector = keyStop[event.which];

  if(selector !== undefined && $(event.target).is(selector)) {
      event.preventDefault(); //stop event
  }
  return true;
 });
});


/**
 * Number.prototype.format(numDecimalDigits)
 * 
 * This breaks the nubmer down into parts. It strips out the
 * sign, the numbers before the first comma, the rest of the 
 * whole number portion, and the decimal part of the answer.
 */
Number.prototype.formatMoney = function(numDecimalDigits) {
	var number = this,
		numDecimalDigits = isNaN(numDecimalDigits) ? 2 : Math.abs(numDecimalDigits),
		thousandSeparator = ',',
		decimalSeparator = ".",
		sign = (number < 0) ? '-' : '',
		integerPart = parseInt(number = Math.abs(number).toFixed(numDecimalDigits)) + '',
		leadingDigits = (leadingDigits = integerPart.length) > 3 ? leadingDigits % 3 : 0;
   return sign + (leadingDigits ? integerPart.substr(0, leadingDigits) + thousandSeparator : "") + 
		integerPart.substr(leadingDigits).replace(/(\d{3})(?=\d)/g, "$1" + thousandSeparator) + 
		(numDecimalDigits ? decimalSeparator + Math.abs(number - integerPart).toFixed(numDecimalDigits).slice(2) : "");
};



</script>

[JavaScript Verification]:
Call Order: After other verification

for(i = 1; i <=3; i++) {
	var questionName = strQuestName + "_MachineChoice_" + i;
	
	var totalPods = 0;
	$("[id^=" + strQuestName + "_Concept" + i + "Pod]").each(function () { totalPods += parseFloat($(this).val()) || 0;})
	

	//If Machine is checked at least one pod must be purchased
	if(SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods <= 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase at least one pod to use the coffee machine you chose.";
	}

	//If a pods is purchased the machine must be checked
	if(!SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods > 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase the machine in order to use the pods you selected.";
	}
	
}

<p>Assuming that you were in the market to purchase a single-serve coffee machine and these were the only products available, which machine or machines would you purchase? (You may review the features of the machines by clicking [% PopUp("here", "Glossary.html", 600, 800) %].)</p>

[HTML <head> Tag]:
<script>	
function SSI_CustomGraphicalCheckbox(GraphicalCheckboxObj, InputObj, blnCheck) {
	var price = parseFloat($(InputObj).closest("div").find("h4").text().replace(/\$/g, ''))
	if(blnCheck) {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) + price;
	} else {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) - price;
	}
	$("#machineTotalPrice").text("$" + SSI_PriceFormat(newPrice, ",", ".").toString())

}

function updatePodPrices() {
	
	var spend = new Array();
	
	$.each($(":text"), function(index, value) {
		var quantity = parseFloat(($(value).val()));
		var price = parseFloat($(value).closest("li").find("input:hidden").val());
		spend[index] = quantity*price;
	});
	
	var totalSpend = 0;

	$.each(spend, function(index, value) {
		if(!isNaN(value)) {
			totalSpend += value;
		}
	});
	
	$("#podsTotalPrice").text("$" + totalSpend.formatMoney(",", ".", 2));
	
}

$(document).ready(function() {$(":text").change(updatePodPrices)})

$(function(){
 var keyStop = {
   8: ":not(input:text, textarea, input:file, input:password)", // stop backspace = back
   13: "input:text, input:password", // stop enter = submit 

   end: null
 };
 $(document).bind("keydown", function(event){
  var selector = keyStop[event.which];

  if(selector !== undefined && $(event.target).is(selector)) {
      event.preventDefault(); //stop event
  }
  return true;
 });
});


/**
 * Number.prototype.format(numDecimalDigits)
 * 
 * This breaks the nubmer down into parts. It strips out the
 * sign, the numbers before the first comma, the rest of the 
 * whole number portion, and the decimal part of the answer.
 */
Number.prototype.formatMoney = function(numDecimalDigits) {
	var number = this,
		numDecimalDigits = isNaN(numDecimalDigits) ? 2 : Math.abs(numDecimalDigits),
		thousandSeparator = ',',
		decimalSeparator = ".",
		sign = (number < 0) ? '-' : '',
		integerPart = parseInt(number = Math.abs(number).toFixed(numDecimalDigits)) + '',
		leadingDigits = (leadingDigits = integerPart.length) > 3 ? leadingDigits % 3 : 0;
   return sign + (leadingDigits ? integerPart.substr(0, leadingDigits) + thousandSeparator : "") + 
		integerPart.substr(leadingDigits).replace(/(\d{3})(?=\d)/g, "$1" + thousandSeparator) + 
		(numDecimalDigits ? decimalSeparator + Math.abs(number - integerPart).toFixed(numDecimalDigits).slice(2) : "");
};



</script>

[JavaScript Verification]:
Call Order: After other verification

for(i = 1; i <=3; i++) {
	var questionName = strQuestName + "_MachineChoice_" + i;
	
	var totalPods = 0;
	$("[id^=" + strQuestName + "_Concept" + i + "Pod]").each(function () { totalPods += parseFloat($(this).val()) || 0;})
	

	//If Machine is checked at least one pod must be purchased
	if(SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods <= 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase at least one pod to use the coffee machine you chose.";
	}

	//If a pods is purchased the machine must be checked
	if(!SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods > 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase the machine in order to use the pods you selected.";
	}
	
}

<p>Assuming that you were in the market to purchase a single-serve coffee machine and these were the only products available, which machine or machines would you purchase? (You may review the features of the machines by clicking [% PopUp("here", "Glossary.html", 600, 800) %].)</p>

You can select a combination of pods, coffee shop purchases and home brew machines if that is what you would actually do. (Note that some of the coffee pods are only available for certain machines.) </p>

[HTML <head> Tag]:
<script>	
function SSI_CustomGraphicalCheckbox(GraphicalCheckboxObj, InputObj, blnCheck) {
	var price = parseFloat($(InputObj).closest("div").find("h4").text().replace(/\$/g, ''))
	if(blnCheck) {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) + price;
	} else {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) - price;
	}
	$("#machineTotalPrice").text("$" + SSI_PriceFormat(newPrice, ",", ".").toString())

}

function updatePodPrices() {
	
	var spend = new Array();
	
	$.each($(":text"), function(index, value) {
		var quantity = parseFloat(($(value).val()));
		var price = parseFloat($(value).closest("li").find("input:hidden").val());
		spend[index] = quantity*price;
	});
	
	var totalSpend = 0;

	$.each(spend, function(index, value) {
		if(!isNaN(value)) {
			totalSpend += value;
		}
	});
	
	$("#podsTotalPrice").text("$" + totalSpend.formatMoney(",", ".", 2));
	
}

$(document).ready(function() {$(":text").change(updatePodPrices)})

$(function(){
 var keyStop = {
   8: ":not(input:text, textarea, input:file, input:password)", // stop backspace = back
   13: "input:text, input:password", // stop enter = submit 

   end: null
 };
 $(document).bind("keydown", function(event){
  var selector = keyStop[event.which];

  if(selector !== undefined && $(event.target).is(selector)) {
      event.preventDefault(); //stop event
  }
  return true;
 });
});


/**
 * Number.prototype.format(numDecimalDigits)
 * 
 * This breaks the nubmer down into parts. It strips out the
 * sign, the numbers before the first comma, the rest of the 
 * whole number portion, and the decimal part of the answer.
 */
Number.prototype.formatMoney = function(numDecimalDigits) {
	var number = this,
		numDecimalDigits = isNaN(numDecimalDigits) ? 2 : Math.abs(numDecimalDigits),
		thousandSeparator = ',',
		decimalSeparator = ".",
		sign = (number < 0) ? '-' : '',
		integerPart = parseInt(number = Math.abs(number).toFixed(numDecimalDigits)) + '',
		leadingDigits = (leadingDigits = integerPart.length) > 3 ? leadingDigits % 3 : 0;
   return sign + (leadingDigits ? integerPart.substr(0, leadingDigits) + thousandSeparator : "") + 
		integerPart.substr(leadingDigits).replace(/(\d{3})(?=\d)/g, "$1" + thousandSeparator) + 
		(numDecimalDigits ? decimalSeparator + Math.abs(number - integerPart).toFixed(numDecimalDigits).slice(2) : "");
};



</script>

[JavaScript Verification]:
Call Order: After other verification

for(i = 1; i <=3; i++) {
	var questionName = strQuestName + "_MachineChoice_" + i;
	
	var totalPods = 0;
	$("[id^=" + strQuestName + "_Concept" + i + "Pod]").each(function () { totalPods += parseFloat($(this).val()) || 0;})
	

	//If Machine is checked at least one pod must be purchased
	if(SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods <= 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase at least one pod to use the coffee machine you chose.";
	}

	//If a pods is purchased the machine must be checked
	if(!SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods > 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase the machine in order to use the pods you selected.";
	}
	
}

[HTML <head> Tag]:
<script>	
function SSI_CustomGraphicalCheckbox(GraphicalCheckboxObj, InputObj, blnCheck) {
	var price = parseFloat($(InputObj).closest("div").find("h4").text().replace(/\$/g, ''))
	if(blnCheck) {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) + price;
	} else {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) - price;
	}
	$("#machineTotalPrice").text("$" + SSI_PriceFormat(newPrice, ",", ".").toString())

}

function updatePodPrices() {
	
	var spend = new Array();
	
	$.each($(":text"), function(index, value) {
		var quantity = parseFloat(($(value).val()));
		var price = parseFloat($(value).closest("li").find("input:hidden").val());
		spend[index] = quantity*price;
	});
	
	var totalSpend = 0;

	$.each(spend, function(index, value) {
		if(!isNaN(value)) {
			totalSpend += value;
		}
	});
	
	$("#podsTotalPrice").text("$" + totalSpend.formatMoney(",", ".", 2));
	
}

$(document).ready(function() {$(":text").change(updatePodPrices)})

$(function(){
 var keyStop = {
   8: ":not(input:text, textarea, input:file, input:password)", // stop backspace = back
   13: "input:text, input:password", // stop enter = submit 

   end: null
 };
 $(document).bind("keydown", function(event){
  var selector = keyStop[event.which];

  if(selector !== undefined && $(event.target).is(selector)) {
      event.preventDefault(); //stop event
  }
  return true;
 });
});


/**
 * Number.prototype.format(numDecimalDigits)
 * 
 * This breaks the nubmer down into parts. It strips out the
 * sign, the numbers before the first comma, the rest of the 
 * whole number portion, and the decimal part of the answer.
 */
Number.prototype.formatMoney = function(numDecimalDigits) {
	var number = this,
		numDecimalDigits = isNaN(numDecimalDigits) ? 2 : Math.abs(numDecimalDigits),
		thousandSeparator = ',',
		decimalSeparator = ".",
		sign = (number < 0) ? '-' : '',
		integerPart = parseInt(number = Math.abs(number).toFixed(numDecimalDigits)) + '',
		leadingDigits = (leadingDigits = integerPart.length) > 3 ? leadingDigits % 3 : 0;
   return sign + (leadingDigits ? integerPart.substr(0, leadingDigits) + thousandSeparator : "") + 
		integerPart.substr(leadingDigits).replace(/(\d{3})(?=\d)/g, "$1" + thousandSeparator) + 
		(numDecimalDigits ? decimalSeparator + Math.abs(number - integerPart).toFixed(numDecimalDigits).slice(2) : "");
};



</script>

[JavaScript Verification]:
Call Order: After other verification

for(i = 1; i <=3; i++) {
	var questionName = strQuestName + "_MachineChoice_" + i;
	
	var totalPods = 0;
	$("[id^=" + strQuestName + "_Concept" + i + "Pod]").each(function () { totalPods += parseFloat($(this).val()) || 0;})
	

	//If Machine is checked at least one pod must be purchased
	if(SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods <= 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase at least one pod to use the coffee machine you chose.";
	}

	//If a pods is purchased the machine must be checked
	if(!SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods > 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase the machine in order to use the pods you selected.";
	}
	
}

[HTML <head> Tag]:
<script>	
function SSI_CustomGraphicalCheckbox(GraphicalCheckboxObj, InputObj, blnCheck) {
	var price = parseFloat($(InputObj).closest("div").find("h4").text().replace(/\$/g, ''))
	if(blnCheck) {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) + price;
	} else {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) - price;
	}
	$("#machineTotalPrice").text("$" + SSI_PriceFormat(newPrice, ",", ".").toString())

}

function updatePodPrices() {
	
	var spend = new Array();
	
	$.each($(":text"), function(index, value) {
		var quantity = parseFloat(($(value).val()));
		var price = parseFloat($(value).closest("li").find("input:hidden").val());
		spend[index] = quantity*price;
	});
	
	var totalSpend = 0;

	$.each(spend, function(index, value) {
		if(!isNaN(value)) {
			totalSpend += value;
		}
	});
	
	$("#podsTotalPrice").text("$" + totalSpend.formatMoney(",", ".", 2));
	
}

$(document).ready(function() {$(":text").change(updatePodPrices)})

$(function(){
 var keyStop = {
   8: ":not(input:text, textarea, input:file, input:password)", // stop backspace = back
   13: "input:text, input:password", // stop enter = submit 

   end: null
 };
 $(document).bind("keydown", function(event){
  var selector = keyStop[event.which];

  if(selector !== undefined && $(event.target).is(selector)) {
      event.preventDefault(); //stop event
  }
  return true;
 });
});


/**
 * Number.prototype.format(numDecimalDigits)
 * 
 * This breaks the nubmer down into parts. It strips out the
 * sign, the numbers before the first comma, the rest of the 
 * whole number portion, and the decimal part of the answer.
 */
Number.prototype.formatMoney = function(numDecimalDigits) {
	var number = this,
		numDecimalDigits = isNaN(numDecimalDigits) ? 2 : Math.abs(numDecimalDigits),
		thousandSeparator = ',',
		decimalSeparator = ".",
		sign = (number < 0) ? '-' : '',
		integerPart = parseInt(number = Math.abs(number).toFixed(numDecimalDigits)) + '',
		leadingDigits = (leadingDigits = integerPart.length) > 3 ? leadingDigits % 3 : 0;
   return sign + (leadingDigits ? integerPart.substr(0, leadingDigits) + thousandSeparator : "") + 
		integerPart.substr(leadingDigits).replace(/(\d{3})(?=\d)/g, "$1" + thousandSeparator) + 
		(numDecimalDigits ? decimalSeparator + Math.abs(number - integerPart).toFixed(numDecimalDigits).slice(2) : "");
};



</script>

[JavaScript Verification]:
Call Order: After other verification

for(i = 1; i <=3; i++) {
	var questionName = strQuestName + "_MachineChoice_" + i;
	
	var totalPods = 0;
	$("[id^=" + strQuestName + "_Concept" + i + "Pod]").each(function () { totalPods += parseFloat($(this).val()) || 0;})
	

	//If Machine is checked at least one pod must be purchased
	if(SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods <= 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase at least one pod to use the coffee machine you chose.";
	}

	//If a pods is purchased the machine must be checked
	if(!SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods > 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase the machine in order to use the pods you selected.";
	}
	
}

<p>Assuming that you were in the market to purchase a single-serve coffee machine and these were the only products available, which machine or machines would you purchase? (You may review the features of the machines by clicking [% PopUp("here", "Glossary.html", 600, 800) %].)</p>
<p>Please also indicate how many of each coffee pods or other cups of coffee you and members of your household would <span class="emphasis">consume</span> in a typical week. You can select a combination of pods, coffee shop purchases and home brew machines if that is what you would actually do. (Note that some of the coffee pods are only available for certain machines.) </p>
<p>Based on your answer to a previous question we estimate that you would have spent about <span style="text-decoration: underline">$[% FormatNumber(HeavyConsumption*0.65, ",", ".", 2)  %]</span> to purchase coffee using a pod based system on a week you drank more coffee than normal. </p>

				<li>[% CBCDesignLevelText(CoffeeCBCHidden_Random9, 1, 2) %]</li>

				<li>[% CBCDesignLevelText(CoffeeCBCHidden_Random9, 1, 4) %]</li>

[HTML <head> Tag]:
<script>	
function SSI_CustomGraphicalCheckbox(GraphicalCheckboxObj, InputObj, blnCheck) {
	var price = parseFloat($(InputObj).closest("div").find("h4").text().replace(/\$/g, ''))
	if(blnCheck) {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) + price;
	} else {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) - price;
	}
	$("#machineTotalPrice").text("$" + SSI_PriceFormat(newPrice, ",", ".").toString())

}

function updatePodPrices() {
	
	var spend = new Array();
	
	$.each($(":text"), function(index, value) {
		var quantity = parseFloat(($(value).val()));
		var price = parseFloat($(value).closest("li").find("input:hidden").val());
		spend[index] = quantity*price;
	});
	
	var totalSpend = 0;

	$.each(spend, function(index, value) {
		if(!isNaN(value)) {
			totalSpend += value;
		}
	});
	
	$("#podsTotalPrice").text("$" + totalSpend.formatMoney(",", ".", 2));
	
}

$(document).ready(function() {$(":text").change(updatePodPrices)})

$(function(){
 var keyStop = {
   8: ":not(input:text, textarea, input:file, input:password)", // stop backspace = back
   13: "input:text, input:password", // stop enter = submit 

   end: null
 };
 $(document).bind("keydown", function(event){
  var selector = keyStop[event.which];

  if(selector !== undefined && $(event.target).is(selector)) {
      event.preventDefault(); //stop event
  }
  return true;
 });
});


/**
 * Number.prototype.format(numDecimalDigits)
 * 
 * This breaks the nubmer down into parts. It strips out the
 * sign, the numbers before the first comma, the rest of the 
 * whole number portion, and the decimal part of the answer.
 */
Number.prototype.formatMoney = function(numDecimalDigits) {
	var number = this,
		numDecimalDigits = isNaN(numDecimalDigits) ? 2 : Math.abs(numDecimalDigits),
		thousandSeparator = ',',
		decimalSeparator = ".",
		sign = (number < 0) ? '-' : '',
		integerPart = parseInt(number = Math.abs(number).toFixed(numDecimalDigits)) + '',
		leadingDigits = (leadingDigits = integerPart.length) > 3 ? leadingDigits % 3 : 0;
   return sign + (leadingDigits ? integerPart.substr(0, leadingDigits) + thousandSeparator : "") + 
		integerPart.substr(leadingDigits).replace(/(\d{3})(?=\d)/g, "$1" + thousandSeparator) + 
		(numDecimalDigits ? decimalSeparator + Math.abs(number - integerPart).toFixed(numDecimalDigits).slice(2) : "");
};



</script>

[JavaScript Verification]:
Call Order: After other verification

for(i = 1; i <=3; i++) {
	var questionName = strQuestName + "_MachineChoice_" + i;
	
	var totalPods = 0;
	$("[id^=" + strQuestName + "_Concept" + i + "Pod]").each(function () { totalPods += parseFloat($(this).val()) || 0;})
	

	//If Machine is checked at least one pod must be purchased
	if(SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods <= 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase at least one pod to use the coffee machine you chose.";
	}

	//If a pods is purchased the machine must be checked
	if(!SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods > 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase the machine in order to use the pods you selected.";
	}
	
}

[HTML <head> Tag]:
<script>	
function SSI_CustomGraphicalCheckbox(GraphicalCheckboxObj, InputObj, blnCheck) {
	var price = parseFloat($(InputObj).closest("div").find("h4").text().replace(/\$/g, ''))
	if(blnCheck) {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) + price;
	} else {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) - price;
	}
	$("#machineTotalPrice").text("$" + SSI_PriceFormat(newPrice, ",", ".").toString())

}

function updatePodPrices() {
	
	var spend = new Array();
	
	$.each($(":text"), function(index, value) {
		var quantity = parseFloat(($(value).val()));
		var price = parseFloat($(value).closest("li").find("input:hidden").val());
		spend[index] = quantity*price;
	});
	
	var totalSpend = 0;

	$.each(spend, function(index, value) {
		if(!isNaN(value)) {
			totalSpend += value;
		}
	});
	
	$("#podsTotalPrice").text("$" + totalSpend.formatMoney(",", ".", 2));
	
}

$(document).ready(function() {$(":text").change(updatePodPrices)})

$(function(){
 var keyStop = {
   8: ":not(input:text, textarea, input:file, input:password)", // stop backspace = back
   13: "input:text, input:password", // stop enter = submit 

   end: null
 };
 $(document).bind("keydown", function(event){
  var selector = keyStop[event.which];

  if(selector !== undefined && $(event.target).is(selector)) {
      event.preventDefault(); //stop event
  }
  return true;
 });
});


/**
 * Number.prototype.format(numDecimalDigits)
 * 
 * This breaks the nubmer down into parts. It strips out the
 * sign, the numbers before the first comma, the rest of the 
 * whole number portion, and the decimal part of the answer.
 */
Number.prototype.formatMoney = function(numDecimalDigits) {
	var number = this,
		numDecimalDigits = isNaN(numDecimalDigits) ? 2 : Math.abs(numDecimalDigits),
		thousandSeparator = ',',
		decimalSeparator = ".",
		sign = (number < 0) ? '-' : '',
		integerPart = parseInt(number = Math.abs(number).toFixed(numDecimalDigits)) + '',
		leadingDigits = (leadingDigits = integerPart.length) > 3 ? leadingDigits % 3 : 0;
   return sign + (leadingDigits ? integerPart.substr(0, leadingDigits) + thousandSeparator : "") + 
		integerPart.substr(leadingDigits).replace(/(\d{3})(?=\d)/g, "$1" + thousandSeparator) + 
		(numDecimalDigits ? decimalSeparator + Math.abs(number - integerPart).toFixed(numDecimalDigits).slice(2) : "");
};



</script>

[JavaScript Verification]:
Call Order: After other verification

for(i = 1; i <=3; i++) {
	var questionName = strQuestName + "_MachineChoice_" + i;
	
	var totalPods = 0;
	$("[id^=" + strQuestName + "_Concept" + i + "Pod]").each(function () { totalPods += parseFloat($(this).val()) || 0;})
	

	//If Machine is checked at least one pod must be purchased
	if(SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods <= 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase at least one pod to use the coffee machine you chose.";
	}

	//If a pods is purchased the machine must be checked
	if(!SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods > 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase the machine in order to use the pods you selected.";
	}
	
}

[HTML <head> Tag]:
<script>	
function SSI_CustomGraphicalCheckbox(GraphicalCheckboxObj, InputObj, blnCheck) {
	var price = parseFloat($(InputObj).closest("div").find("h4").text().replace(/\$/g, ''))
	if(blnCheck) {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) + price;
	} else {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) - price;
	}
	$("#machineTotalPrice").text("$" + SSI_PriceFormat(newPrice, ",", ".").toString())

}

function updatePodPrices() {
	
	var spend = new Array();
	
	$.each($(":text"), function(index, value) {
		var quantity = parseFloat(($(value).val()));
		var price = parseFloat($(value).closest("li").find("input:hidden").val());
		spend[index] = quantity*price;
	});
	
	var totalSpend = 0;

	$.each(spend, function(index, value) {
		if(!isNaN(value)) {
			totalSpend += value;
		}
	});
	
	$("#podsTotalPrice").text("$" + totalSpend.formatMoney(",", ".", 2));
	
}

$(document).ready(function() {$(":text").change(updatePodPrices)})

$(function(){
 var keyStop = {
   8: ":not(input:text, textarea, input:file, input:password)", // stop backspace = back
   13: "input:text, input:password", // stop enter = submit 

   end: null
 };
 $(document).bind("keydown", function(event){
  var selector = keyStop[event.which];

  if(selector !== undefined && $(event.target).is(selector)) {
      event.preventDefault(); //stop event
  }
  return true;
 });
});


/**
 * Number.prototype.format(numDecimalDigits)
 * 
 * This breaks the nubmer down into parts. It strips out the
 * sign, the numbers before the first comma, the rest of the 
 * whole number portion, and the decimal part of the answer.
 */
Number.prototype.formatMoney = function(numDecimalDigits) {
	var number = this,
		numDecimalDigits = isNaN(numDecimalDigits) ? 2 : Math.abs(numDecimalDigits),
		thousandSeparator = ',',
		decimalSeparator = ".",
		sign = (number < 0) ? '-' : '',
		integerPart = parseInt(number = Math.abs(number).toFixed(numDecimalDigits)) + '',
		leadingDigits = (leadingDigits = integerPart.length) > 3 ? leadingDigits % 3 : 0;
   return sign + (leadingDigits ? integerPart.substr(0, leadingDigits) + thousandSeparator : "") + 
		integerPart.substr(leadingDigits).replace(/(\d{3})(?=\d)/g, "$1" + thousandSeparator) + 
		(numDecimalDigits ? decimalSeparator + Math.abs(number - integerPart).toFixed(numDecimalDigits).slice(2) : "");
};



</script>

[JavaScript Verification]:
Call Order: After other verification

for(i = 1; i <=3; i++) {
	var questionName = strQuestName + "_MachineChoice_" + i;
	
	var totalPods = 0;
	$("[id^=" + strQuestName + "_Concept" + i + "Pod]").each(function () { totalPods += parseFloat($(this).val()) || 0;})
	

	//If Machine is checked at least one pod must be purchased
	if(SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods <= 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase at least one pod to use the coffee machine you chose.";
	}

	//If a pods is purchased the machine must be checked
	if(!SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods > 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase the machine in order to use the pods you selected.";
	}
	
}

<p>Assuming that you were in the market to purchase a single-serve coffee machine and these were the only products available, which machine or machines would you purchase? (You may review the features of the machines by clicking [% PopUp("here", "Glossary.html", 600, 800) %].)</p>

You can select a combination of pods, coffee shop purchases and home brew machines if that is what you would actually do. (Note that some of the coffee pods are only available for certain machines.) </p>

			$resultString = $resultString."\t\t<input name='CBCRandom".$taskNum."_Concept".$concept."PriceForPod$i' id='CBCRandom".$taskNum."_Concept".$concept."PriceForPod$i' type='hidden' value='$podPrice'></li>\n";
			$i++;
		}
		return $resultString

		End Unverified %]
	</ul>

[HTML <head> Tag]:
<script>	
function SSI_CustomGraphicalCheckbox(GraphicalCheckboxObj, InputObj, blnCheck) {
	var price = parseFloat($(InputObj).closest("div").find("h4").text().replace(/\$/g, ''))
	if(blnCheck) {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) + price;
	} else {
		var newPrice = parseFloat($("#machineTotalPrice").text().replace(/\$/g, '')) - price;
	}
	$("#machineTotalPrice").text("$" + SSI_PriceFormat(newPrice, ",", ".").toString())

}

function updatePodPrices() {
	
	var spend = new Array();
	
	$.each($(":text"), function(index, value) {
		var quantity = parseFloat(($(value).val()));
		var price = parseFloat($(value).closest("li").find("input:hidden").val());
		spend[index] = quantity*price;
	});
	
	var totalSpend = 0;

	$.each(spend, function(index, value) {
		if(!isNaN(value)) {
			totalSpend += value;
		}
	});
	
	$("#podsTotalPrice").text("$" + totalSpend.formatMoney(",", ".", 2));
	
}

$(document).ready(function() {$(":text").change(updatePodPrices)})

$(function(){
 var keyStop = {
   8: ":not(input:text, textarea, input:file, input:password)", // stop backspace = back
   13: "input:text, input:password", // stop enter = submit 

   end: null
 };
 $(document).bind("keydown", function(event){
  var selector = keyStop[event.which];

  if(selector !== undefined && $(event.target).is(selector)) {
      event.preventDefault(); //stop event
  }
  return true;
 });
});


/**
 * Number.prototype.format(numDecimalDigits)
 * 
 * This breaks the nubmer down into parts. It strips out the
 * sign, the numbers before the first comma, the rest of the 
 * whole number portion, and the decimal part of the answer.
 */
Number.prototype.formatMoney = function(numDecimalDigits) {
	var number = this,
		numDecimalDigits = isNaN(numDecimalDigits) ? 2 : Math.abs(numDecimalDigits),
		thousandSeparator = ',',
		decimalSeparator = ".",
		sign = (number < 0) ? '-' : '',
		integerPart = parseInt(number = Math.abs(number).toFixed(numDecimalDigits)) + '',
		leadingDigits = (leadingDigits = integerPart.length) > 3 ? leadingDigits % 3 : 0;
   return sign + (leadingDigits ? integerPart.substr(0, leadingDigits) + thousandSeparator : "") + 
		integerPart.substr(leadingDigits).replace(/(\d{3})(?=\d)/g, "$1" + thousandSeparator) + 
		(numDecimalDigits ? decimalSeparator + Math.abs(number - integerPart).toFixed(numDecimalDigits).slice(2) : "");
};



</script>

[JavaScript Verification]:
Call Order: After other verification

for(i = 1; i <=3; i++) {
	var questionName = strQuestName + "_MachineChoice_" + i;
	
	var totalPods = 0;
	$("[id^=" + strQuestName + "_Concept" + i + "Pod]").each(function () { totalPods += parseFloat($(this).val()) || 0;})
	

	//If Machine is checked at least one pod must be purchased
	if(SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods <= 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase at least one pod to use the coffee machine you chose.";
	}

	//If a pods is purchased the machine must be checked
	if(!SSI_GetValue(questionName) && totalPods > 0 ) {
		strErrorMessage = "You must purchase the machine in order to use the pods you selected.";
	}
	
}
